	TUR_send_slavs_to_serbia = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_political_discourse
		allowed = {
			original_tag = TUR
		}
		cost = 15
		state_target = yes
		targets = {
			105
			761
			760
			104
			107
			809
			876
			821
		}
		on_map_mode = map_only
		days_remove = 35
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = TUR_can_expel_serbs_to_serbia
			controls_state = FROM
			FROM = {
				has_state_flag = TUR_southslav_state
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_southslav_minority }
			}
		}
		available = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					country_exists = SER
					SER = {
						any_owned_state = {
							is_core_of = SER
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					country_exists = MNT
					MNT = {
						any_owned_state = {
							is_core_of = MNT
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = {
				TUR_target_state_manpower = state_population
			}
			divide_temp_variable = {
				TUR_target_state_manpower = -5
			}
			add_manpower = var:TUR_target_state_manpower
		}
		remove_effect = {
			FROM = {
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_southslav_minority }
				clr_state_flag = TUR_southslav_state
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							is_core_of = TUR
						}
					}
					add_core_of = TUR
				}
				set_state_flag = TUR_unintended_consequence_violence_in_serbia
			}
			random_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_owned_by = SER
							is_controlled_by = SER
							is_core_of = SER
						}
						AND = {
							is_owned_by = MNT
							is_controlled_by = MNT
							is_core_of = MNT
						}
					}
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					TUR_target_state_manpower = -1
				}
				add_manpower = var:TUR_target_state_manpower
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = TUR_violence_in_serbia_flag
					}
					add_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = TUR_violence_in_state
						days = 30
					}
				}
				ottoman_minority_variable_check = yes
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				FROM = {
					any_neighbor_state = {
						has_state_flag = TUR_ottoman_minority_state
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				FROM = {
					any_neighbor_state = {
						any_country = {
							has_war_with = TUR
							controls_state = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

			tag = TUR
		}
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				tag = ITA
			}
		}
		available = {

				is_in_faction = no

					is_in_faction = no
				}
				has_global_flag = kis_firstbalkan_war
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = italo_turkish_war
			NOT = {
 				has_country_flag = ITA_libyan_war_mission_timeout
 				has_global_flag = italo_turkish_war_ends
 			}
 			if = {
 				limit = {
 					has_global_flag = kis_war
 				}
 				OR = {
 					has_global_flag = great_war_ends
 					NOT = {
 						is_in_faction_with = FRA
 						is_in_faction_with = GER
 						has_war_with = FRA
 						has_war_with = GER
 					}
 				}
 			}
			owns_state = 448
			owns_state = 450
			owns_state = 661
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				has_war_with = ITA
				OR = {
					casualties > 50000
					ITA = {
						controls_state = 448
						controls_state = 450
						controls_state = 661
						controls_state = 663
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = BUL
					has_war_with = SER
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 500
				has_war_with = BUL
				has_war_with = SER
				has_war_with = ITA
				ITA = {
					surrender_progress < 0.05
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			ITA = {
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_italianturkish.4
				}
			}
		}
	}

					amount = 5000
					producer = FROM
				}
			}

			}
		}

		fire_only_once = no
		days_remove = 180
		days_re_enable = 30
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = ENG
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			production_speed_industrial_complex_factor = 0.02
		}
		remove_effect = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = TUR

						building = industrial_complex
						size > 0
						include_locked = yes
					}
				}
				add_building_construction = {

TUR_reclaiming_ahd_i_milli = {
	TUR_border_skirmishes = {
		icon = border_war

		target_array = neighbors

		available = {
			FROM = {
				any_owned_state = {
					is_controlled_by = FROM
					any_neighbor_state = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
						set_temp_variable = { var:attacker_state_temp = id }
						has_ROOT_at_least_1_div_in_current_state_scope = yes
						hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_state_flag = border_incident_active } }
					}
					NOT = { has_state_flag = border_incident_active }
					set_temp_variable = { var:defender_state_temp = id }
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_non_aggression_pact_with = FROM }
		}

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = TUR_disobey_the_treaties
			FROM = { exists = yes }
			NOT = { has_war_with = FROM }
			FROM = { has_not_initiated_border_incident_with_ROOT = yes }
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				is_subject_of = FROM
			}

			NOT = { has_border_war_with = FROM }
			FROM = {
				any_owned_state = {
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
					hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_state_flag = border_incident_active } }
					any_neighbor_state = {
						hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_state_flag = border_incident_active } }
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
		}

		cost = 50

		fire_only_once = no

		days_remove = 7
		days_re_enable = 15

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				FROM = {
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						limit = {
							is_claimed_by = ROOT
							hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_state_flag = border_incident_active } }
							any_neighbor_state = {
								hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_state_flag = border_incident_active } }
								has_ROOT_at_least_1_div_in_current_state_scope = yes
								is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							}
						}
						save_event_target_as = defender_state
						set_variable = { FROM.defender_state_vs_@ROOT = id }
						set_temp_variable = { defender_state_temp = id }
						set_state_flag = border_incident_active
					}
				}
				random_state = {
					limit = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
						hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_state_flag = border_incident_active } }
						has_ROOT_at_least_1_div_in_current_state_scope = yes
						any_neighbor_state = {
							state = var:FROM.defender_state_vs_@ROOT
						}
					}
					save_event_target_as = attacker_state
					set_variable = { FROM.attacker_state_vs_@ROOT = id }
					set_temp_variable = { attacker_state_temp = id }
					set_state_flag = border_incident_active
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			start_border_war = {
				change_state_after_war = yes
				attacker = {
					state = var:FROM.attacker_state_vs_@ROOT
					num_provinces = 4
					on_win = wtt_border_conflict_won_attacker.1
					on_lose = wtt_border_conflict_lost_attacker.1
					on_cancel = wtt_border_conflict_canceled_attacker.1
				}
				
				defender = {
					state = var:FROM.defender_state_vs_@ROOT
					num_provinces = 4
					on_win = wtt_border_conflict_won_defender.1
					on_lose = wtt_border_conflict_lost_defender.1
					on_cancel = wtt_border_conflict_canceled_defender.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_border_conflict_defender_vs_FROM = yes }
				var:attacker_state_vs_@FROM = {
					clr_state_flag = border_incident_active
				}
				var:defender_state_vs_@FROM = {
					clr_state_flag = border_incident_active
				}
				clear_variable = attacker_state_vs_@FROM
				clear_variable = defender_state_vs_@FROM
			}
			else = {
				FROM = {
					var:attacker_state_vs_@ROOT = {
						clr_state_flag = border_incident_active
					}
					var:defender_state_vs_@ROOT = {
						clr_state_flag = border_incident_active
					}
					clear_variable = attacker_state_vs_@ROOT
					clear_variable = defender_state_vs_@ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
